<div id="workskin">
  <div class="preface group">
    <h2 class="title heading">
      The Vow
    </h2>
    <h3 class="byline heading">
      <a rel="author" href="/users/Lynansidhe/pseuds/Lynansidhe">Lynansidhe</a>
    </h3>


        <div class="summary module" role="complementary">
          <h3 class="heading">Summary:</h3>
            <blockquote class="userstuff">
              <p>Several key characters from Fairytail travel to Hogwarts to fulfill the ancient vow made by Mavis to protect Hogwarts. Very strong Cobra/Lucy; if you don't like the shipping, I would recommend not reading it. This story is discontinued because I am working to write a better version of this story.</p>
            </blockquote>
        </div>


  </div>


<!--/descriptions-->

<!--chapter content-->
    <div id="chapters" role="article">
        <h3 class="landmark heading" id="work">Work Text:</h3>
          <div class="userstuff"><p>The Vow                                                                                           7-25-15<br/>Chapter One-<br/>Makarov Dreyar, third and sixth guild master of Fairy Tail, sighed wearily as he looked down into his mug; torn upon the decision that was looming over their guild. On one hand he knew what he had to do, it was the other part of him, the piece that loved and cherished his "children" that rebelled against sending his brats into a second land in the throes of chaos and great confusion.<br/>When the ancient lacrima crystal that had been passed down from guild master to guild master began to shine did he begin to dread. Of course, he knew that the day of repaying the debt of the first master would come, but he had hoped that it would be later. Much later. Once more Makarov sighed; he still remembered seeing that lacrima vision when he became third guild master.<br/>________________________________________<br/>'Why does my whole-body ache?' Thought a childlike blonde who was also known as Mavis Vermillion first master and founder of the guild Fairy Tail as she attempted to open her eyes. Then they shot open as she jolted upright only for her body to scream in agony over the motion 'Itai, Itai.' She thought, banging her back into the closest tree; remembering the last words in her conscious before it all went black. ""The air. . ." she gasped, clutching her throat in a desperate attempt to inhale the vital Ethernano particles that configured the very essence of magic. . . " Heart skipping a beat, she sucked in air desperately only to stop in horror. Trying to calm down and use her famous analytical mind, Mavis took in a deep breath ignoring the wrongness, and searched.<br/>'Right, I was talking to Precht-san on Mount Hakobe after we had investigated a disturbance and got rid of the Vulcan's when the ground gave out.' Mavis shuddered at the remembrance of free falling as well as Precht's horrified countenance while he watched helplessly. 'Before I hit the ground I threw myself onto an outcropping; stopping my fall, which explains the pain.' Her brows scrunched together in thought. 'Could this possibly be akin to Edolas? Just another dimension?' Tapping her lips, Mavis's brilliant green eyes narrowed, thinking through all of the possibilities before settling on one. "Something about that rock that I touched must have sent me here. That much I have deduced. I wonder. . . Is there such a place where I have landed? If so. . Then I have my work cut out for me." She mused aloud before firming her resolve "I will not bend nor admit defeat, I must find a way to return! I cannot disappoint my friends!" With determination flowing, Mavis heaved herself upon her feet, feeling every twinge and tear in the bitingly chilly air.<br/>~~~Four Days Later~~~<br/>Gasping as she knelt on the ground, Mavis looked around at the carnage that she had wrought as her arms trembled at the last spec of magic vanished from her soul. "No complaints. Now if you would move over to the first table, we can continue."<br/>"Now where was Iâ€¦?" Horace muttered to himself. "Ahâ€¦ yes. Here I was. Alright, for our second pair, we have Hermione Granger from Gryffindor with Cobra from Slytherin."<br/>'Ehh?' Hermione jumped, and swung her gaze towards a decidedly unhappy Cobra. 'I have to be with him?' She wailed internally. Finding the tall, one-eyed man intimidating despite her decision to be open minded about these transfer students. 'There's just something sinister about him. It gives me the chills.' She rubbed her arms. 'I feel like he is walking over my grave whenever he just passes by me.'<br/>"Trust me on this, Bookworm, I would rather not be with you either." Cobra whispered into her ear, causing her to release an 'eep!' that was muffled by the Slayer's scarred hand.<br/>'How did he get over here so quickly? Or so quietly for that matter?!' The brown-haired Witch panicked.<br/>"But since I have no choice either, I suggest that we work together for this week and try to do well." He continued, releasing his hand from her mouth.<br/>Sending a glare over her shoulder at the tall male, Hermione huffed angrily at his presumptuous attitude and stomped over to the indicated seat and slammed her books down. 'Argh! Insufferable man! Hah! Try to do well! I'll show him!'<br/>Watching the feisty brunette stomp away from him, Cobra felt a smirk grow on his face. 'This is going to be fun.'<br/>-Line Breakâ€”<br/>"Now then," Slughorn clapped his hands together again. "Are we all settled?" Hearing no complaints, the man trudge onward. "Good, good. Today we are going to brew a draught of liquid death." His voice lowered dramatically. "And whoever brews the best batch, will get a small vial of Felix Felicis. Can anyone tell me what this is? Yes, Miss Granger?"<br/>"Felix Felicis, or more communing known as liquid luck, grants the user temporary good fortune. However, if taken too often, it has been known to cause bad luck."<br/>The Professor nodded enthusiastically at her answer, paying no mind to the fact that she had just quoted the book verbatim. "Very nice. Splendid job, Miss Granger! Ten points for Gryffindor."<br/>Hermione all but glowed at the teacher's praise.<br/>"Since Miss Granger answered that question, could anybody tell what is in that cauldron over there?" Slughorn pointed at the gently bubbling pink potion.<br/>When no one answered, he frowned and asked, "Anyone?"<br/>Almost timidly, Hermione raised her hand.<br/>"Miss Granger?"<br/>"It is a love potion sir. And unlike popular myth, it cannot actually make a person fall 'in love' with another. Only make them feel infatuated with the giver."<br/>"Ah, very nice. Another ten points for Gryffindor."<br/>"Thank you, Professor." She murmured.<br/>A few feet away from Hermione, Draco scoffed in disgust. "Stop looking so proud, Mudblood." He sneered. "Anyone could have answered those questions."<br/>Hermione flushed, and started to say something but was interrupted by Cobra's coolly cut voice.<br/>"So why didn't you answer them? Since apparently you know it all."<br/>"Baka..." Cobra added in a mutter.<br/>Draco immediately turned as scarlet as a certain requip mage's hair. "Why youâ€¦ do you know who my father is?"<br/>"Pathetic." Erik sneered, his eye showing nothing but contempt for the blonde.<br/>A brighter red infused Draco's features. This time, however from embarrassment.<br/>"Pathetic." Cobra repeated, derision practically dripping from his voice. "Relying on your father's name to strike fear in people. You're not worth my time."<br/>Turning away, the conversation done in his mind, he called out to the gaping brunette. "Come on Bookworm. We're getting different seats. I refuse to be in the company of such a noxious prat."<br/>Finding an adequate seat in back, Cobra sat down, put his legs on the table and leaned back with his hands behind head and closed his eye; giving off an air of relaxed lethalness.<br/>Meanwhile Hermione stood beside their desk chewing her lip as she tried to gather the courage to say something. Anything.<br/>Cracking open his eye, Cobra startled Hermione by being the first to say something. "Aren't you going to sit?"<br/>"I am. I mean I'm going to." She quickly amended at his sardonic look.<br/>"Well you might want to decide soon. Everyone's waiting." He yawned and shut his eye again.<br/>Hermione looked around and realized, with mortification, that everyone was staring at them and waiting. "Sorry." She muttered, sliding into her seat, her cheeks nearly burgundy.<br/>"It's quite alright, m'dear." Slughorn smiled reassuringly at the girl before going back to his lesson. "Since we are all seated-"<br/>At this comment, Hermione sunk lower into her chair.<br/>"-we can now begin the race to get this prized potion; Felix Felicis." The professor held up the small vial proudly. "Now everyone, get your books out and find the recipe for liquid deathâ€¦ and begin!" He turned over a large hourglass.<br/>Hermione scrambled to turn to the right place- her mind and body in a frenzy. "Cobra, cut the beetle."<br/>When he did not move from his relaxed position, Hermione's temper got the better of her. "What are sitting around for? I said cut the beetle!"<br/>Not even deigning to open his eye, Cobra responded in a dangerously quiet voice. "Do not order me around."<br/>"W-what?" Hermione drew back at the murderous aura pouring off her partner.<br/>"You heard me." He pinned her with an intense glare and then shook his head as if to rid himself of something unpleasant, and swung his feet of the table and stood up. "But since we have a partnership, I will help you. Just don't ever, presume to order me around again. Am I clear?" He enunciated slowly and precisely.<br/>"Crystal."<br/>"Good." Cobra directed his attention to the scrabbling beetle as caught it with one, lightning fast lunge; choosing to ignore the gasp at his sudden movement. "Get everything else ready. I'll finish with this." That said, he then proceeded to crush the insect with the flat of his blade.<br/>"What are you doing?" Hermione asked in horror. "The book says to cut the beetle, not crush it!"<br/>He just gave her a look and continued to crush the beetle.<br/>"Stop! Please." She added when his amethyst orb swung towards her.<br/>"This will get more juice this way."<br/>"Huh?" Hermione blinked in surprise at the random statement. "But the bookâ€¦" She protested weakly when she figured out what Cobra was alluding too.<br/>"Is wrong." Erik dumped the juice into the cauldron and proceeded to stir counterclockwise seven times and clockwise once.<br/>"What are you doing?! You're going to ruin itâ€¦" Hermione moaned.<br/>Cobra rolled his eye. 'So dramatic.' "Have a little faith Bookworm. I know what I'm doing." 'Thanks to that black haired kid's book.'<br/>"But it's wrong! The book says to stir it seven times counterclockwise!"<br/>Completely tuning out the brunette's complaints, Cobra continued to follow the instructions of the late coming Wizard's book instead of his own. 'This makes the potion making easy.' He was brought out of his thoughts by the sound of a cauldron shattering.<br/>Acting on instinct, Cobra spun the stunned witch behind him and absorbed the corrosive concoction flying at them. 'Darn, what was that? It tasted disgusting!' Erik grimaced, rubbing at his mouth. 'But I do feel better. More awake.'<br/>"-bra. Cobra!" Hermione shook his arm for seemed to be hundredth time. She slumped in relief when the glazed over eye became luminous once more. "Thank God! I thought that the potion had blinded you."<br/>"I'm fine." He removed his arm from her grasp. "Did anything hit you?"<br/>She shook her head.<br/>"Good." Erik moved away from Hermione and strode over to the now quivering Neville Longbottom and shaking Ronald Weasley. Coming to a halt in front of the duo, he leveled a menacing glower at them. "You two-" He jabbed an accusing finger. "Are idiots. You could have seriously hurt someone with that explosion."<br/>"It was an accident!" Ron squeaked.<br/>Erik felt himself grow angry at the half truth. Knowing from the ginger's mind that he had not been paying very much attention to his potion and was goofing off. "Liar." He hissed.<br/>"Hey, calm down!" Harry interjected. "Ron said it was an accident! Just let it go!"<br/>About to say something snappy in rebuttal, Cobra was stopped by the surprising arrival of Laxus.<br/>"Well, well, well," Erik drawled slowly. "Look who it is. To what do I owe this honor?"<br/>Casting a look that clearly said knock it off, Laxus replied by saying, "I heard that you were causing trouble."<br/>Erik's eye narrowed before swinging towards Meredy accusingly.<br/>The Maguilty Mage just smile and waved cheerfully.<br/>He growled and stalked out of the room, the Lightning Dragon Slayer following after him smugly.<br/>'I hate them.' Cobra grumbled, paying no mind to the astonished stares he was getting.<br/>But Hermione's stare was for an entirely different reason than the rest. 'I could've sworn I saw the potion hit him. In fact, I'm sure that it did! But how did he get out unscathed?'<br/>________________________________________<br/>After they had walked out of hearing range, Cobra stopped abruptly and turned towards Laxus. "Alright, we're far enough away. What do you really want?"<br/>A Cheshire like grin lit the blonde's face. "Now what makes you think that?"<br/>Looking flatly at Laxus, Erik snorted and pointed at S-Class Mage. "That. Now spill it."<br/>"Punishment." Laxus answered simply.<br/>"For what?" Cobra asked, indignant.<br/>This time it was Laxus's turn to level a flat glare at Cobra. "For skipping patrolling and making Gajeel and me stay up all night covering blondieâ€™s and your shift."<br/>"Whoops. Forgot."<br/>"Well, your 'whoops' caused a lot of danger! And because of that, I'm assigning guard duty for the rest of the week."<br/>"What about Bright Eyes?"<br/>"She'll join you once she wakes up."<br/>"Right." Cobra sighed. Feeling tired already. "When do I start?"<br/>Laxus smirked. "Now."<br/>Erik swore at him as the older Slayer sauntered away. Obviously proud of himself. And the fact the he had just gotten a weeks' vacation. 'Oh, whatever shall I do with all this free time?'<br/>"Temeâ€¦" Cobra growled darkly at retreating back, seriously considering throwing something.<br/>________________________________________<br/>Standing next to Harry and Wendy, Slughorn looked incredulously at their perfect potion. "Merlin's beard! You two got it correct! Two vials of liquid luck for you two!" He handed them each a bottle- which they took very gingerly while Hermione watched with a sullen countenance. Her potion having gone downhill once Cobra left. Her bushier hair than normal testified to that.<br/>'And I was so closeâ€¦'She thought mournfully.<br/>________________________________________<br/>Levy glanced subtly up at the dragon slayer walking next to her and smiled.<br/>"What's wrong, Shrimp?" Gajeel questioned.<br/>"Nothing. Just thinking."<br/>"Don't think too hard!" An annoying voice cackled. "You might hurt your wee~ brain."<br/>"Who's there?" Gajeel stepped defensively in front of Levy.<br/>"Nobody~!"<br/>"Cut the crap! Show yourself!"<br/>"Nope! No can do dragon boy!" The disembodied voice chirped.<br/>Angry tick marks started to appear on Gajeel's face. 'Why thatâ€¦'<br/>"Gajeelâ€¦" Levy laid a hand on his tensed arm. "It's what he wants. So instead, let me do something."<br/>Gajeel looked back at Levy in curiosity. Intrigued despite his desire to protect her.<br/>Stepping out from behind the Slayer, Levy cast several binding spells in quick succession. "Solid Script: Soul Chains! Solid Script: Chains of Visibility!"<br/>The Bluenette twirled her pen smugly when a cursing Poltergeist came crashing to the floor; wrapped from head to toe in glowing chains.<br/>"Nice one, Shrimp." Gajeel complemented, already cracking his knuckles.<br/>"Not so fast, dragon boy!" Peeves cackled as best he could while being chained to the ground. "I know your precious little secret. And you wouldn't want it to, slip out?"<br/>The Slayer paused in mid-step. "What are you talking about?"<br/>Peeves gazed slyly at the black haired Mage. "I know where you're actually from. And if you upset me enough, I might just slip up and forget my little promise to the Word Witch."<br/>"Promise? What promise? Levy?"<br/>"Ooh~ trouble in paradise?" The Poltergeist sniggered.<br/>"Urusai!" Both mages snapped at the same time at the annoying and antagonistic ghost.<br/>Pinching the bridge of her nose, Levy explained everything.<br/>After blinking a few times as he tried to process what had just been said, Gajeel finally said something after about a minute of complete silence. "So that was the reason why you were talking to yourself last night."<br/>'Eh?!' Levy fell to the ground in surprise. 'That's what he got out of that all?!'<br/>As she fell, her focus on her spells vanished and released the now whooping Peeves.<br/>"Ooh~ she released Peevsie!" He cackled manically as he zoomed from one corner to next. "Don't forget about our bargain!" The Poltergeist sang, making one last swoop before completely vanishing to do more mischief.<br/>Up on her feet once more, Levy banged her head against Gajeel's iron hard chest and winched when the pain registered. "Owâ€¦" She rubbed at the forming bump with a grimace.<br/>Gajeel's hands pushed the Bluenette's away and took over rubbing her bruised head for her. "Are you alright Shrimp?"<br/>"Yeah. I'm fine." 'I really shouldn't have done that.'<br/>"Anyway," Levy began in an effort to fill the awkward silence that had descended. "I need to go find a certain talking cat. Want to help me?"<br/>Gajeel shrugged his shoulders. "Got nothing better to do. Which cat are you looking for?"<br/>"Happy." Levy giggled, cracking up at the thought of Carla or Pantherlily acting in cahoots with the Poltergeist.<br/>The Slayer lifted his nose and sniffed the air. "He's this way."<br/>"Thanks Gajeel!" She followed after him, incredibly thankful for dragon slayers with super noses.<br/>He merely grunted in reply; intent on tracking the blue exceed.</p></div>
